    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer18215691850804718088">What happens when an unsuspecting girl and guy are thrown into a marriage they don't want? That's exactly the case of Ivory and Darius, born into different families whose marriage serves to prevent competition between their businesses. No matter how they oppose the idea, their parents are hell-bent on marrying them to each other to honor a five-generation-old deal that too</span>
  <span id="freeText18215691850804718088" style="display:none">What happens when an unsuspecting girl and guy are thrown into a marriage they don't want? That's exactly the case of Ivory and Darius, born into different families whose marriage serves to prevent competition between their businesses. No matter how they oppose the idea, their parents are hell-bent on marrying them to each other to honor a five-generation-old deal that took place between their ancestors. For Ivory, whose heart has just been broken, her marriage to the handsome but cold Darius Quartz fails to provide her the happy life she wants. Instead, she finds herself in endless boredom and doing the same things she'd been doing the past six months. That is, until Darius arrives home from his training and her ex returns in the picture. Thrown in her loyal best friend, Rose, and Darius's insane cousin, Adrian. Her life suddenly turns upside down and becomes exciting and a whole lot crazier! It's a long journey full of tears, fun, joy, even insanity, and most of all, love.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18215691850804718088" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1107616503" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1107616503" />
    <a title="Zara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29040726-zara"><img alt="Zara" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1107616503?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zara" href="/user/show/29040726-zara">Zara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23286464-marriage-by-law">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1107616503" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8830894648912547971">"1.3 stars" <br/>This book was absolutely crappy. The grammar was atrocious. The use of language was terrible. The story was absolutely, completely and utterly predictable. The author had no sense of direction and constantly contradicted herself. <br/>Ivory's character I believe was destined to remain 20 forever. She was 'almost 21' before she got married and even after 6 months spent apart from Darius(her husband) and quite some time spent with him, she still remains 20. I mean girl, if you have the secr</span>
  <span id="freeText8830894648912547971" style="display:none">"1.3 stars" <br />This book was absolutely crappy. The grammar was atrocious. The use of language was terrible. The story was absolutely, completely and utterly predictable. The author had no sense of direction and constantly contradicted herself. <br />Ivory's character I believe was destined to remain 20 forever. She was 'almost 21' before she got married and even after 6 months spent apart from Darius(her husband) and quite some time spent with him, she still remains 20. I mean girl, if you have the secret to immortality then you gotta share. Her age does however thankfully change during the epilogue. <br />Also we get the impression that Darius is a spoilt dumb blonde(figure of speech people, no offense intended). He wears dress shoes and suits to beaches, has no idea what cotton candy or a carnival is (I mean do you honestly expect us to believe this shit?) and despite being a hard core businessman, cannot tie a tie(this is clearly the result of amnesia after marriage since he was always impeccably dressed when he was at odds with his wife). <br />Also what is the deal with James(the ex)? At the start of the book, he's a poor orphan (she believed this for four years while they were together) and then suddenly, he's the son of a rich socialite( Seriously?!) Hes also ugly, skinny, insecure, dresses like a pimp, drowns himself in cologne and has no self respect or class. And yet you still loved him and were with him for four years you miserable hypocrite (aren't you the bitter ex)! And I won't even try and explain what's going on with their parents. You're probably smart enough to figure that out if you're unfortunate enough to read the book... or not. <br />Half of the story is spent bullshitting the readers. Do you really expect us to believe that she was married to a guy for six months and still didn't know what he looked like (note increasing crappiness). <br />Also, if they're so rich, why do Adrian and Ivory eat like impoverished street urchins. Add to that the fact that the romance is spectacularly unbelievable (writing such a lifeless romance takes mad skills ladies and gentlemen 4) and the characters have the maturity and emotional depth of cardboard. <br />Nonetheless, I somehow slogged through this miserable excuse for a book in the hopes of finding a saving grace as indicated by the rave reviews. I was however severely disappointed and obviously misdirected by several wattpad fans of this book who wouldn't know a good book if it hit them in the face while tied to an anvil. As for the person who gave this book '1.5 frustrating stars', I say amen to that sister. Had I listened to you, I wouldn't have wasted hours of my life reading this monstrosity.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8830894648912547971" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Kristine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7277619-kristine"><img alt="Kristine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415716652p2/7277619.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristine" href="/user/show/7277619-kristine">Kristine</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1015128803" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer18318212940725194203"><br/>I finished this in just one sitting! I love the pacing because it's very realistic unlike other stories that the guy and girl fell instantly. There are "no" unnecessary dramas. Just the right amount of it. I would like to read more of this author's work. <br/><br/>How I wish to meet someone like "Dairy" who's a bit snobbish in the beginning. So far, this is the best realistic/contemporary story I've read this year. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1576692822?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angel" href="/user/show/26294860-angel">Angel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1576692822" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12705910895685344722">Now normally if I don't finish a book, I don't rate it as I think it's unfair but this time I have no choice but to give it a 1 star rating to reduce the average rating. This book has an average rating of 4.37 which really, really baffles me. It's misleading and by rating and writing this review I hope to stop my fellow readers from falling into the same trap as me.<br/>The main character, Ivory, is ridiculous. She's 20 but you would never tell from her behavior. My four year old cousin is more matur</span>
  <span id="freeText12705910895685344722" style="display:none">Now normally if I don't finish a book, I don't rate it as I think it's unfair but this time I have no choice but to give it a 1 star rating to reduce the average rating. This book has an average rating of 4.37 which really, really baffles me. It's misleading and by rating and writing this review I hope to stop my fellow readers from falling into the same trap as me.<br />The main character, Ivory, is ridiculous. She's 20 but you would never tell from her behavior. My four year old cousin is more mature! She's from this affluent family and has been getting 'lady' lessons yet she didn't even have basic manners or etiquette. Her husband is apparently some hot-shot CEO but he has just finished his degree, like just right now. Okay, okay, let's assume he is some business protege or was born with an amazing business acumen and he doesn't need a measly degree to become a CEO, then why the hell is he so damn stupid?! He doesn't know what a carnival is, what candy floss is and never seen a sausage roll before. Where has he been living - under a rock? He leaves his wife with a guy who is obviously a pervert, I thought businessmen had a good sense of judgement? <br />And lastly the premise. I am a fan of arranged / contract / marriage of convenience but their reasons for getting married was just absurd!<br />Please save yourself frustration and multiple WTF's per page and just skip this book. Don't let the average rating suck you in! I repeat, don't fall for it!</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1079071575" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1079071575" />
    <a title="Dijya " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13019542-dijya"><img alt="Dijya " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597738514p2/13019542.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1079071575?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dijya " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dijya " href="/user/show/13019542-dijya">Dijya </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23286464-marriage-by-law">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1079071575" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer164043070483765987"><b>
  <i>**1.5 Frustrated Stars**</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>This book was my first by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8380012.N_K__Pockett' title='N.K. Pockett' rel='nofollow noopener'>N.K. Pockett</a> and to say I just picked it up randomly would be a lie. I liked its blurb and was really excited to read it as it was obvious it's HEA and what could go wrong with a HEA, right?<br/>Nope, definitely wrong!<br/><br/>I couldn't even wrap my mind around some of the moments in this book and most of the time I kept thinking of DNFing it but hey I still finished it..Yay to me!!<br/><br/>I liked the beginning of the book and it captured my interest for a while </i></span>
  <span id="freeText164043070483765987" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>**1.5 Frustrated Stars**</i>
</b><br><br><i>This book was my first by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8380012.N_K__Pockett" title="N.K. Pockett" rel="nofollow noopener">N.K. Pockett</a> and to say I just picked it up randomly would be a lie. I liked its blurb and was really excited to read it as it was obvious it's HEA and what could go wrong with a HEA, right?<br>Nope, definitely wrong!<br><br>I couldn't even wrap my mind around some of the moments in this book and most of the time I kept thinking of DNFing it but hey I still finished it..Yay to me!!<br><br>I liked the beginning of the book and it captured my interest for a while there but by sixth chapter I was seriously getting frustrated. The hold their parents had on both of them was seriously getting on my nerves.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413297686ra/11491701.gif" width="300" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As theirs was not a marriage of love so I was hoping for laughing moments or casual bickering hell even fighting would have been okay but indifference towards each other for so long, made me bored.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413297686ra/11491702.gif" width="300" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wouldn't say I hated Ivory but I didn't like her either. Yeah, she mentioned she used to be a headstrong girl but how could you suppress your nature completely.<br><br>She couldn't even stand up to her mother who in fact was a robot or seems so, I didn't like her too not even a little bit but why am I giving her any importance by mentioning her? Okay, back to the main point..Ivory didn't want to get married but because of the circumstances she couldn't deny her mother.<br><br>Darius, the king of nonchalance, okay not the king but he totally owned the title for 5-6 chapters. Trusting your wife is one thing and leaving her alone with some creep while off to complete your ‘Important’ work is downright insulting. He certainly was not going to make to my BBF’s list by then.Even now he’s nowhere near the top ones but by the end at least I was able to stand him.<br><br>Darius came home after six months of their marriage and both of them didn’t have any kind of contact between them in those months.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413297686ra/11491703.gif" width="300" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After coming back home, what made him decide to go on a vacation was not elaborated but you didn't hear me complaining.<br>For me their time together alone was sounding a promising one and it was turning out to be and I would be honest I was seriously hoping for a more get to know each other with some steamy sexy scenes but Nope..nada not even a single kiss by then..:(<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406546884ra/10564409.gif" width="175" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>To say I was disappointed would be an understatement and what was more unexpected was for their parents to be at their cottage out of the blue trying to check out the situation between them and once again controlling their lives.<br><br>Ivory was taught to act like a lady, sure, but there has to be limit for everything. You can’t ask your daughter to just get up and be reading for a ball, fever be damned.<br><br>Adrian was Darius’s cousin and I liked him for some part of the book. Though Ivory’s friend Rose was mentioned in the book but she wasn’t being involved by author much and frankly most of the time I forgot about her.<br><br>I tried reading every line believe me I did but some of the pages still get flipped with only the dialogues being read.<br><br>I certainly would not be reading any more books by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8380012.N_K__Pockett" title="N.K. Pockett" rel="nofollow noopener">N.K. Pockett</a> at least not anytime soon. Maybe I’ll read the next book by her.<br>Though I’m not gonna recommend this book to anyone but if you wanna try it, go for it.<br>Hope you enjoy it ♥♥</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="164043070483765987" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1091671079" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1091671079" />
    <a title="CasPerfitz~SLiTsReaD" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9406114-casperfitz-slitsread"><img alt="CasPerfitz~SLiTsReaD" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455478450p2/9406114.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1091671079?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="CasPerfitz~SLiTsReaD" class="user" itemprop="url" name="CasPerfitz~SLiTsReaD" href="/user/show/9406114-casperfitz-slitsread">CasPerfitz~SLiTsReaD</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23286464-marriage-by-law">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1091671079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5478275916178318467">4 Sweet and Entertaining Stars!<br/><br/>I thought this was quite a fun and enjoyable read. As long as you don’t over analyze all the details of the story and just enjoy the ride… ;)<br/><br/>It starts with Ivory finding out that her boyfriend has been cheating on her all the time. Brokenhearted and all, enters her overbearing mother who forces her to marry Darius to prevent competition between their businesses and to honor a five-generation-old deal that took place between their ancestors. In other word, it’s an a</span>
  <span id="freeText5478275916178318467" style="display:none">4 Sweet and Entertaining Stars!<br /><br />I thought this was quite a fun and enjoyable read. As long as you don’t over analyze all the details of the story and just enjoy the ride… ;)<br /><br />It starts with Ivory finding out that her boyfriend has been cheating on her all the time. Brokenhearted and all, enters her overbearing mother who forces her to marry Darius to prevent competition between their businesses and to honor a five-generation-old deal that took place between their ancestors. In other word, it’s an arrange marriage between business rivals. ;)<br /><br />To cut the story short, she married Darius, their marriage started off cold, then they started spending time together and got to know each other, and got closer… Then her douche of an ex returns in the picture… add to the equation her crazy BFF, Rose, and, last but not the least, Darius insanely funny cousin Adrian… Ivory’s supposedly boring life just got more crazier and exciting! <br /><br />I really enjoyed the humour of the story… Ivory has a very likeable character… she is born rich but is down to earth and unspoiled. Darius on the other hand I thought was a lost cause in the beginning, but then there are hints that he is more than what meets the eye. It’s too bad that I am not able to read Darius POV or get to know him more. He is, to the end, still a mystery.. But, despite all that, I find myself warming up to him. <br /><br />But Adrian, Darius cousin, really stole most of the show here. I thought he was hilarious. I find myself enjoying Ivy and Adrian’s antics, I thought they were amusing. <br /><br />It is entertaining. I thought it was sweet, funny and endearing.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5478275916178318467" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2394771594" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2394771594" />
    <a title="Aya Hamza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11660871-aya-hamza"><img alt="Aya Hamza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1575410515p2/11660871.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<div id="review_2035448501" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2035448501" />
    <a title="Holmahaff" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31297962-holmahaff"><img alt="Holmahaff" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399901309p2/31297962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2035448501?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Holmahaff" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Holmahaff" href="/user/show/31297962-holmahaff">Holmahaff</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2035448501" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17579828747359924587">I couldn't finish this book. It was just too unrealistic. Wannabe perfect heroine with all the qualities seemingly just so “trying to be Mr. Darcy” could fall for her.<br/>I read it because it had so good rating and I understand that some people may like it, but for me it was just.. Bad. <br/> <br/>Spoilers!<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><u>Pros</u><br/>-That these people don’t exist.. Okay I’m joking… or am I? <br/>-Yeah yeah nice of them to gradually fall in love yada yada yada.<br/>- some funny moments<br/> <br/>And now everyone’s favorite:<br/> <br/><u>Cons</u><br/>-how can be with someone</span>
  <span id="freeText17579828747359924587" style="display:none">I couldn't finish this book. It was just too unrealistic. Wannabe perfect heroine with all the qualities seemingly just so “trying to be Mr. Darcy” could fall for her.<br />I read it because it had so good rating and I understand that some people may like it, but for me it was just.. Bad. <br /> <br />Spoilers!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><u>Pros</u><br />-That these people don’t exist.. Okay I’m joking… or am I? <br />-Yeah yeah nice of them to gradually fall in love yada yada yada.<br />- some funny moments<br /> <br />And now everyone’s favorite:<br /> <br /><u>Cons</u><br />-how can be with someone for 4 YEARS and know NOTHING about them..<br />-The reason for why they had to get married was just ridiculous... I mean wtf??<br />- Ivory says in the beginning that it's the 21. century, thank you Ivory for letting us know, if you hadn’t I would have thought it was set in the fucking middle ages, forced marriage and all that shit. <br />- Darius was really just a jerk sometimes, I am tired of authors making excuses for bad behavior in heroes for just being “misunderstood”. I thought it very immature of him to act the way he did, just be nice to people, it’s not that hard.<br />- Just Ivory’s character! Her constant eye rolling, childish behavior, her going to med school and yet she couldn’t say <b>hypothermia</b>… I mean sorry but I’m not buying it that you have been studying your ass off to go to med school but still say <b>hyperthemicia</b>, and of course fucking Darius had it right (because he is perrrrfect). I also felt her constant jabbering about her being the best in every sport very tiresome and it was like the author was saying: my heroine is beautiful, hot, clever (going to med school (hah you wish), really cool because she plays every sport and played hockey with the boys for four years, strong minded and... did I mention cool? I felt all these qualities were only there so fucking Darius would fall in love with her. And why is she telling us all these things? That’s because nearly nothing in the character's behavior suggests it. If Ivory is so strong minded why can’t she just tell her family to hire some lawyers and find another less medieval way of having good relationship between companies or why did she not just keep studying for med school? Who says that marrying a CEO would mean being a 18th century housewife. But no, the author thinks she is a feminist by making her character stubborn and childish, because that my friend is sexy version of feminists ;)<br />-The fucking seafood, just fucking say: I’m sorry, this all looks very nice but I’m allergic to seafood. Just lie Ivory goddammit! It would have spared so many the agony of reading about it. <br />- The spineless dad, you don’t do stuff like this to your children <br />-The mother, why did she act like she did?? There must be a reason! (maybe there is an heartfelt moment later in the book where the woman explains why she hates her daughter, but I wouldn’t know, I gave up)<br />- Sentences like: I thought dad had the pants in the family.. Just don’t<br /> <br />Thank you for reading this review. I’m sorry if there are some grammar mistakes in here, English is my second language.I also didn’t finish the book so maybe some of the things I complained about improved later on. <br /> <br />Have a wonderful day!<br /> <br />P.s also if you would like to read a good romance that is sweet but not crap &lt;:^) <br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29364480.The_Bookshop_on_the_Corner" title="The Bookshop on the Corner by Jenny Colgan" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bookshop on the Corner</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17579828747359924587" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer774846620180299124">6/5 stars ( it deserves a million)<br/><br/>Whilst there are some negative views on this book below - regarding "1.5 frustrated stars" I think the person who wrote that review has is stupid, or has not read the book - as they themselves said they brushed over it. <br/><br/>The best part about the story was that it was a change, perfect for a cold winter day, with a hot drink cuddling up and dreaming we could get our own Darius. <br/><br/>The slow pace was realistic, it was not like every other novel where the man says I love</span>
  <span id="freeText774846620180299124" style="display:none">6/5 stars ( it deserves a million)<br /><br />Whilst there are some negative views on this book below - regarding "1.5 frustrated stars" I think the person who wrote that review has is stupid, or has not read the book - as they themselves said they brushed over it. <br /><br />The best part about the story was that it was a change, perfect for a cold winter day, with a hot drink cuddling up and dreaming we could get our own Darius. <br /><br />The slow pace was realistic, it was not like every other novel where the man says I love you and gets her in bed by the 3rd chapter, no, sure it takes half the novel for them to finally kiss, but it's beautiful. When they kiss you cry and feel it in your bones. When they smile, your stomach flips and the cute moments are enough to make you wish that men like Darius existed. <br /><br />I think whoever wrote that 1.5 review is utter bullshit and should be shamed to write a review AFTER saying them self that they didn't read the book thoroughly, of course one is states to their own opinion but that was just a horrible review black marking this novel that deserved much more credit. <br /><br />Compared to other novels, this one is utterly beautiful <br /><br />It is not about two people trying to change each other, its about acceptance.<br />It really shows how you should be yourself and people will love you for who you are, even though it takes time, after all apples don't grow on trees overnight.<br /><br />To be brutally honest, I would recommend this book to anyone, and I really think you should read this beautiful novel. </span>

  <span id="freeText8664963930830600778" style="display:none">I felt like this was the longest book EVER. I did not care for the way the author skipped from Present to Past over and over again.               <span id="reviewTextContainer2654584259" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3157198057586750911">Not one to really give a book such few stars but I felt this book really just waffled on. Giving it 2 stars as there was some funny moments (thanks to Adrian). I finished reading it as I was waiting for something to happen...but Ivory just slept and ate her way through the entire book.   <span id="freeText3157198057586750911" style="display:none">Not one to really give a book such few stars but I felt this book really just waffled on. Giving it 2 stars as there was some funny moments (thanks to Adrian). I finished reading it as I was waiting for something to happen...but Ivory just slept and ate her way through the entire book. This story had a lot of potential but no background was explored... author should have gone more in depth into Ivory and her mother's relationship. More background on this business rivalry and deal (and by the way not once is it mentioned how they are rich - they just are...hm ok). More on Ivory and Darius getting close to one another. Loads of typo mistakes. I got really bored towards the end when I realised the plot wasn't going to pick up. The pool table scene was just unnecessary long. The amount of times she gets hit on... (rolling my eyes) and the amount to junk food consumed throughout the book... rather unrealistic. This was a big no-no for me. Quite surprised it has high reviews.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7431618997707256877">Actually, it was a strange story and difficult to rate.<br/>The pair started off as complete strangers, forced to marry and caring nothing for each other.<br/>As time went by, they had to live together and learn to be intimate. It wasn't easy at all.<br/>The most bizarre thing in this book is that, while both of them are very young (21,25), sex is out of the question. Why?   <span id="freeText7431618997707256877" style="display:none">Actually, it was a strange story and difficult to rate.<br />The pair started off as complete strangers, forced to marry and caring nothing for each other.<br />As time went by, they had to live together and learn to be intimate. It wasn't easy at all.<br />The most bizarre thing in this book is that, while both of them are very young (21,25), sex is out of the question. Why? Apart from very few kisses, they seem almost victorian. How can this happen in a contemporary romance?<br />Could it be that the author is a prude, maybe too religious? I hope not because, if it is so, I'll stay away from her books in the future.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14072977506721508031">Read this book on wattpad.<br/>I loved probably all of the characters and the development of the relationship between Darius and Ivory at the perfect pace which the majority of romance books fail to get right because it either drags or is unrealistic.<br/>It wasn't a tense read but it was humorous and adorable with the way Darius, Ivory and Adrian interacted. The personality of the characters remained constant and stood out. <br/>It was a light read and I would definitely recommend this book.</span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GPleOr4YIEN6c6bPZj8rFDS8u+hxm7IpbJVzo1YzGbD3w4hJ//EMNC2oa7KlXFGsYnUTBXbS4F1An8yBvGNnJQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('uSPymHvPnNtp5r559+h00mfXXy4x4dw7K/sWQSi19YlWGSTrOiawrD49cwQ0iw5qMR73wzaojk8H8aljwuWLHA==')})
  }
